\bentry
\word[U(1)]{U}
\pron{yU}
\gl{\nA}
\expl{(\bava\ \eng{Us} yA \eng{U's} )}
\bmng
(\eng{u} eMdU \parx) 
\bnum
\num{1}iMgilxSf vaNaRmAleya ipapxtotxMdaneya akaSxra. 
\num{2} \eng{U} AkArada vasutx yA vakarx(reVKe) (\kanmu\ \saMpa gaLalilx baLake): \eng{U-bolt.} 
\enum
\emng
\eentry

\bentry
\word[U(2)]{U} 
\pron{U} 
\gl{\nA}
\expl{}
\bmng
(bamiVRyaralilx) obabxna hesarina muMde seVrisuva gwravasUcaka birudu. 
\emng
\eentry

\bentry

\pron{yU} 
\gl{\gu}
\expl{}
\bmng
(\kanmu\ \birx)

\num{2} meVluvagaRda vishiSaTx lakaSxNa eMdu naMbalAda. 
\enum
\emng
\eentry

\bentry
\word[U(4)]{U} 
\pron{yU} 
\gl{\saMkiSx}
\expl{}
\bmng

\num{2} \eng{University}.

\pron{yUbikivxTi} 
\gl{\nA}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum

\emng

\noindent

\expl{}
\bmng

\num{3} huTeTxV ilalxda; eMdeMdigU huTuTx paDeyada: \eng{unborn hopes} huTeTxV paDeyada niriVkeSxgaLu.

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\eng{unconscious humour} arivilalxda hAsayx. 
\emng
\eentry

\bentry
\word[unconscious(2)]{unconscious} 
\pron{anfkAnaSxsf} 
\gl{\nA}
\expl{}
\bmng
 (\mavi) (manasisxna) aparxjecnx; supatx, ajAgaqta -- sithxti; jAgaqta manasisxge nilukada, Adare naDavaLike, BAvagaLu, \mo vugaLa meVle pariNAma biVruva manasisxna viBAga: \eng{collective unconscious} samaSiTx supatxparxjecnx. 
\emng
\eentry

\gl{\nA}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum

\alnum{b} aBayxMjana, leVpana -- vasutx; teYla \mo vu. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{2} (\rUpa) shAmaka, sAMtavxnada, samAdhAnakAraka -- nuDi, AloVcane, vicAra. 
\numi{3} 
\banum
\alnum{a}(dhAmiRkoVtAsxha, dhAmiRka saMsAkxra, gADhaBAvane, \mo vugaLiMda uMTAguva) mAtina yA daniya -- mAdaRva, nuNupu, naya. 
\alnum{b} iMtahudara toVrike; kaqtaka naya; beNeNxyaMtha nayagArike. 
\eanum

\bentry
\word[under(1)]{under} 
\pron{aMDarf}
\gl{\upa}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} keLage; keLagaDe: \eng{it fell under the table} adu meVjina keLage bitutx. \eng{under the left eye} eDagaNiNxna keLage. 
\num{2} keLage; aDiyalilx; taLagaDe; bauDadalilx: \eng{under the high wall} A etatxrada goVDeya bauDadalilx. \eng{under the cliff} kaDidAda baMDeya keLage. 
\num{3} hiMdugaDe; hiMBAgadalilx; mareyalilx: \eng{under the island} divxVpada hiMdugaDe. 
\num{4} oLage; oLagaDe; taLagaDe: \eng{inserted a knife under the bark} togaTeya oLage oMdu cUriyanunx cucicxda. \eng{wore a vest under his shirt} SaTiRna oLage vesfTx toTiTxdadx. 
\num{5} keLadajeRya; keLagina: \eng{no one under a bishop} obabx biSapfgiMta keLagina dajeRyavaru yArU ilalx. 
\num{6} kaDame KaciRnalilx, vecacxdalilx: \eng{under Rs. 4000} nAlukx sAvira rUpAyi gaLigiMta kaDame KaciRnalilx. 
\num{7} oLagAgi; sikikx; adhiVnavAgi; oLapaTuTx; IDAgi; anuBavisutatx: \eng{sank under the load} BAradiMda keLage kusiyitu. \eng{groaning under tyranny} dabAbxLikege sikikx naraLutatx. \eng{is under repair} durasitxyalilxde. 
\num{8} peYru -- neTiTxruva, hAkiruva: \eng{50 acres under wheat} aivatutx ekarege goVdhi hAkidudx. 
\num{9} (yAvudoV iMdhanashakitx \mo vugaLiMda) muMdakekx calisutatx; dUDalAgutatx: \eng{under sail} hAyi (paTada) neraviniMda muMdakekx calisutatx. 
\num{10} (\pArxparx) (obabxra adhikaqta ruju, muderx, keYbareha, \mo vugaLiMda) (\kanmu) daqDhiVkarisida; parxmANa mADida: \eng{under one's hand and seal} tAneV rujumADi muderx otitxda. 
\num{11} saradiya parxkAra inonxbabx (isipxVTu) ATagArananunx -- anusarisutatx, hiMbAlisutatx. 
\num{12} keLage; vagaRdalilx; guMpinalilx; vagiRVkaraNagoMDu: \eng{that book goes under biology} A pusatxka jiVvavijAcnxnada keLage barutatxde. \eng{goes under many names} halavAru hesarugaLalilx ide. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\hyperdef{U}{under(1)pagu}{} 
\bnum
\num{1} \eng{take under one's} \hyperref{kandict_w.pdf}{W}{wing(1) pagu(8)}{$^1$wing}. 
\num{2} \eng{under a} \hyperref{kandict_c.pdf}{C}{cloud(1) nuga(2)}{$^1$cloud}. 
\num{3} \eng{under} \hyperref{kandict_a.pdf}{A}{age(1) pagu(5)}{$^1$age}. 
\num{4} \eng{under} \hyperref{kandict_a.pdf}{A}{arm(2) nuga(4)}{$^2$arms}. 
\num{5} \eng{under} \hyperref{kandict_c.pdf}{C}{convas(1) pagu(1)}{$^1$canvas}. 
\num{6} \eng{under} \hyperref{kandict_c.pdf}{C}{control(1) pagu(3)}{$^1$control}. 
\num{7}\eng{under} \hyperref{kandict_c.pdf}{C}{cover(2) pagu(3)}{$^2$cover}. 
\num{8} \eng{under} \hyperref{kandict_f.pdf}{F}{fire(1) pagu(9)}{$^1$fire}. 
\num{9} \eng{under} \hyperref{kandict_f.pdf}{F}{foot(1) nuga(37)}{$^1$foot}. 
\num{10} \eng{under one's} \hyperref{kandict_a.pdf}{A}{arm(1) pagu(2)}{$^1$arm}. 
\num{11} \eng{under one's} \hyperref{kandict_b.pdf}{B}{belt(1) nuga(4)}{$^1$belt}. 
\num{12} \eng{under one's} \hyperref{kandict_b.pdf}{B}{breathpagu(13)}{breath}. 
\num{13} \eng{under one's} \hyperref{kandict_h.pdf}{H}{hat(1) nuga(15)}{$^1$hat}. 
\num{14} \eng{under} \hyperref{kandict_h.pdf}{H}{hatch(1) pagu(2)}{$^1$hatches}. 
\num{15}\eng{under person's} \hyperref{kandict_n.pdf}{N}{nose(1) pagu(29)}{$^1$nose}.

(\kanmu\ daqDhamanasisxniMda) anuBavisu; IDAgu; oLagAgu; sahisu; paDu: \eng{has undergone many trials} aneVka kelxVshagaLanunx sahisidAdxne, anuBavisidAdxne. \eng{undergo an operation} shasatxrXcikitesxge oLagAgu. 
\emng
\eentry

\bentry
\word{understand} 
\pron{aMDarfsATxYxMDf}
\gl{\kirx}
\expl{(\BU\ matutx \BUkaq\ \eng{understood} \ucAcx-- aMDarfsuTxDf). }


\noindent
\gl{\sakirx}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} (mAtugaLu, vayxkitx, BASe, \mo vugaLa) athaR -- garxhisu, hiDi; athaRmADiko; ari(tuko); tiLi(duko): \eng{does not understand what you say} niVnu heVLuvudu(avanige) athaRvAguvudilalx. \eng{understands you perfectly} ninanxnunx pUNaRvAgi aritukoMDidAdxne. \eng{cannot understand French} pherxMcfBASeyanunx athaRmADikoLaLxlAra. 
\num{2} (udedxVsha, vivaraNe yA kAraNavanunx) garxhisu; ari; tiLi; Uhisu; gotutx mADiko; athaR mADiko: \eng{do not understand why he came} avanu yAke baMdanoV nanage tiLiyadu. \eng{could not understand what the noise was about} A galATe yAvudara bagegx eMbaudu gotAtxgalilalx. \eng{do not understand the point of his remark} avana TiVkeya aMshavanunx nAnu athaRmADikoLaLxlAre. 
\num{3} (yAvudAdarU sUcane yA mAhitiya AdhArada meVle Uhe, tiVmARna, \mo vugaLige baruvalilx) naMbau; eNisu; Uhisu; BAvisu; takiRsu: \eng{I understand that it begins at noon} adu madhAyxhanx pArxraMBavAgutatxdeMdu nananx Uhe. \eng{I understand that expenses were to be paid} KacuRmADiruvudanunx tuMbikoDalAgutatxdeMdu nAnu eNisutetxVne. 
\num{4} (AshacxyaR, koVpa, saMdeVha, \mo vanunx sUcisuvAga) tiLi; garxhisu; aMduko: \eng{am I to understand that you refuse?} niVnu nirAkarisutitxVyeMdu tiLiyaleV? 
\num{5} (manasisxnalilx) (padavanunx) adhAyxhAra mADiko: \eng{the verb may be either expressed or understood} kirxyApada vAcayxvAgirabahudu yA adhAyxhAravAgirabahudu. 
\num{6} lakaSxNa yA savxBAvavanunx sahAnuBUtiyiMda -- athaRmADiko, tiLi, gamanisu, aritiru: \eng{quite understand your difficulty} ninanx kaSaTx nanage athaRvAgutatxde (nAnu balelx). \eng{cannot understand him at all} avananunx athaRmADikoLuLxvudeV kaSaTx. 
\num{7}(heVge nivaRhisabeVkeMbaudanunx, vayxvaharisabeVkeMbaudanunx) aritiru; athaRmADikoMDiru: \eng{could never understand algebra} biVjagaNitavanunx eMdU athaRmADikoLaLxlAgiradavanAgidedx. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\akirx}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} (sAmAnayxvAgi yA vishiSaTx athaRdalilx) athaRvAgu; arivAgu. 
\num{2} (UheyiMda yA Kacita AdhArada meVle) tiLi; garxhisu; naMbau: \eng{he is coming to -- morrow, I understand} (avanu nALe barutAtxneMdu keVLide, hwde?) avanu nALe barutitxdAdxneMdu tiLididedxVne. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} \hyperref{kandict_g.pdf}{G}{give(1) pagu(16)}{$^1$give} \eng{person to understand.} 
\num{2} \eng{tongue not understanded of the people} (\pArxparx) janakekx athaRvAgadidadx paricayavilalxdidadx BASe, anayxBASe, paraBASe. 
\numi{3} \eng{understand each other} 
\banum
\alnum{a} obabxrigobabxru athaRmADikoLiLx; parasapxrara aBipArxya, BAvane, \mo vanunx garxhisikoLiLx. 
\alnum{b} parasapxra omamxtadalilxri yA oLasaMcinalilx BAgigaLAgiri. 
\eanum
\numie
\enum
\emng

\pron{anfphoVlfDx}
\gl{\sakirx}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} maDikegaLanunx bicucx; padaragaLanunx tege; maDike teredu haravu. 
\num{2} vikAsagoLisu: \eng{the story unfolds itself} kathe vikAsagoLuLxtAtx hoVgutatxde. 
\num{3} (AloVcanegaLu, haMcike, \mo vanunx) bayalumADu; parxkaTagoLisu; horageDavu: \eng{she unfolded her plans} avaLu tananx yoVjanegaLanunx horageDavidaLu. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent 
\gl{\akirx}
\expl{}
\bmng
araLu; vikAsavAgu; bicicxko; tereduko. 
\emng
\eentry

\expl{}
\bmng
(\BUvi) EkarUpa parxkirxyA -- sidAdhxMta, vAda; BUveYjAcnxnika parxkirxyegaLu satatavAgi matutx aviratavAgi parxyoVgavAgutitxruva balagaLa pariNAma eMba sidAdhxMta yA vAda. 
\emng
\eentry

\bentry
\word{uniformity} 
\pron{yUniphAmiRTi} 
\gl{\nA}
\expl{(\bava\ \eng{uniformities}). }
\bmng
oMdeV samanAgiruvudu; EkariVtiyAgiruvudu; EkaparxkArate; EkarUpate; EkakarxmAnusaraNe. 
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\eng{Act of Uniformity} (\ca) cacuRgaLa pArxthaRnAvidhigaLalilx EkarUpate taralu, sAmAnayx pArxthaRneya nidiRSaTx pusatxkavanunx baLasalu iMgelxMDinalilx 1662ralilx mADida shAsana, masUde. 
\emng
\eentry

\bentry
\word{union} 
\pron{yUnayxnf, yUnianf} 
\gl{\nA}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} okakxTuTx; okUkxTa; aikayx; seVrike; saMyoVga: \eng{the union of the parts was imperfect} BAgagaLa seVrike asamapaRkavAgitutx. 
\num{2} maduve; vivAha (saMbaMdha): \eng{a happy union} suKavAda vivAha saMbaMdha. 
\num{3} hoMdike; sAmarasayx; sAMgatayx; meYtirx; EkiVBAva: \eng{lived together in perfect union} saMpUNaRvAda meYtirxyiMda oMdAgi jiVvana naDesidaru. 
\numi{4} (vividha BAgagaLu seVri racitavAgiruva) rAjakiVya okUkxTa: 
\banum
\alnum{a} (\kanmu) amerikada saMyukatx saMsAthxnagaLu. 
\alnum{b} gerxVTf birxTanf matutx \kanu\ aileRMDu. 
\alnum{c} dakiSxNa Aphirxkada okUkxTa. 
\alnum{d} soVviyeTf okUkxTa. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{5} (\ga) kUTa; eraDu athavA hecucx gaNa \eng{(set)} gaLige seVrida elalx dhAtugaLanUnx oLagoMDa motatx. 
\num{6} saMGa; saMGaTane; aMgaBAgagaLu yA sadasayxru parasapxra kUDi racitavAda okUkxTada vayxvasethx. 
\numi{7} 
\banum
\alnum{a} (\ca) pAyxriSf kUTa; saMyukatx pAyxriSf; nigaRtikara jiVvanAdhAra kAnUnugaLa nivARhakAkxgi oMdugUDisida halavu pAyxriSfgaLu. 
\hypertarget{union(7)b}{} 
\alnum{b} iMtha saMyukatx pAyxriSf sAthxpisida UT-vasati odagisuva, nigaRtikara Alaya; anAthAlaya. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{8} (\birx) (sahakArakAkxgi) oMdugUDisida cacuRgaLa kUTa. 
\numi{9} 
\banum
\alnum{a} (vishavxvidAyxnilayada yA kAleVjina) vidAyxthiR saMGa yA cacARsaMGa: \eng{the debate at the Oxford union} AkfsxphaDfR vidAyxthiRsaMGadalilx naDeda cacARkUTa. 
\alnum{b} iMtha saMGada vasati kaTaTxDagaLu. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{10} gerxVTf birxTaninxna dhavxjadalilx (rUDhiyAgi dhavxjasatxMBada magugxlina meVlu mUleyalilx kANuva) okUkxTa cihenx. 
\num{11} (koLave \mo vugaLanunx sulaBavAgi kUDisalu yA beVpaRDisalu baLasuva) joVDaNe salakaraNe; saMyoVjaka. \imglink{union 11.:fig}{\raisebox{-0.15cm}[0pt][0pt]{\pdfimage width 0.5cm height 0.5cm {U_Pictures/union.jpg}}} 
\num{12} (hatitx, linanf, reVSemx yA seNbau, \mo vugaLa) misharx neyegx baTeTx. 
\numi{13} 
\banum
\alnum{a} ogUgxDike; saMyoVjane; saMGaTane; oMdugUDuvudu. 
\alnum{b} ogUgxDida sithxti; saMyukatx sithxti; saMGaTita sithxti. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{14} vaqtitx saMGa; vaqtitxnirataru, kAmiRkaru tamamx aBivaqdithx matutx hitarakaSxNegAgi EpaRDisikoMDa okUkxTa. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent 
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\numi{1} \eng{the Union} 
\banum
\alnum{a} saMyukatx rAjayx, rASaTxrX; 1603ralilx iMgelxMDu matutx sAkxTelxMDugaLa okUkxTa. 
\alnum{b} 1801ralilx gerxVTf birxTanf matutx airelxMDugaLa okUkxTa. 
\alnum{c} 1707ralilx iMgelxMDina hAgU sAkxTelxMDina pAliRmeMTugaLa okUkxTa. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{2} \eng{union down} (vipatitxna sUcaneyAgi) okUkxTa cihenx keLage baruvaMte hArisida bAvuTa; talekeLagAgi hArisida bAvuTa. 
\enum
\emng

\gl{\nA}

\bmng

\eanum
\numie
\num{2} (\saM) kUDugAyana yA kUDuvAdana; savxrameVLa yA vAdayxmeVLa; oMdeV shurxtiyalilxruva yA aSaTxmasavxradiMda badalAguva oMdu yA hecicxna shurxtigaLalilxruva kaMThagaLu yA vAdayxgaLu parasapxra hoMdikeyAguvaMte saMyoVgavAguvudu, meVLeYsuvudu: \eng{sang in unison} kUDugAyanadalilx hADidaru. 
\num{3} sAmarasayx; hoMdike; sAMgatayx; meVLa: \eng{acted in perfect unison} (elalxroDane) saMpUNaR sAmarasayxdiMda naDedukoMDa. 
\enum

\bentry
\word{unit} 
\pron{yUniTf} 
\gl{\nA}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\numi{1} 
\banum
\alnum{a} oMdu; Eka; EkAMsha; GaTaka; \kanmu\ lekAkxcAradalilx `oMdu' eMbaudAgi gaNisuva biDi matutx pUNaR vasutx, vayxkitx, athavA avugaLa yA avara taMDa. 
\alnum{b} EkAMsha; oMdu saMkiVNaR aKaMDadalilx seVriruva ati cikakxdAda biDi vayxkitxgaLalilx, vasutxgaLalilx yA guMpugaLalilx parxti oMdu: \eng{the family as the unit of society} samAjada GaTaka, (EkAMsha)veMdu parigaNisida kuTuMba. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{2} `oMdu' eMba saMKeyx. 
\num{3} (itara motatxgaLanunx nideRVshisalu parxmANavAgi tegedukoLuLxva) EkamAna: \eng{unit of heat} tApada EkamAna. \eng{mass per unit volume} oMdu Gana aLate EkAMshakekx, EkamAnakekx iruva darxvayxrAshi. 
\num{4} (viduyxcaPxkitx \mo vugaLige dara vidhisuvAga gaNisuva) EkamAna. 
\num{5} yUniTf TarxsfTxna atayxMta kaniSaThxvAda SeVru. 
\num{6} (saMkiVNaRvAda oMdu yaMtarxracaneyalilx vishiSaTxvAda kelasakAkxgi niyoVjisida, Adare oTuTx yaMtarxda BAgavAda) biDi salakaraNe. 
\num{7} (adaraMteyeV iruva, uLidavugaLoDane hoMdikoLaLxleMdu niyoVjisalAda yA oMdara pUraka BAgagaLalilx oMdAgi racisida) piVThoVpakaraNa. 
\num{8} (oMdu saMsethxyalilx) GaTaka; visheVSa taMDa; vishiSaTxvAda kelasakekxMdu udedxVshisalAda guMpu yA taMDa. 
\enum
\emng

\num{3} aikayxte; sAMgatayx; sAmaMjasayx; aMgaBAgagaLa ucitavAda parasapxra saMbaMdha yA hoMdike: \eng{the picture lacks unity} I citarxdalilx aikayxte, sAMgatayx ilalx. 
\num{4} vayxSiTx: aKaMDa samagarxvAgiruva saMkiVNaR vasutx: \eng{a person regarded as a unity} aKaMDa samagarxvAgi pariBAvitanAgiruva vayxkitx. 
\num{5} (\ga) oMdu; Eka. 
\num{6} (vayxkitxgaLu \mo vara naDuvaNa) hoMdike; sAmarasayx; omamxnasusx: \eng{dwell together in unity} oMdAgi bALu. 
\num{7} ogagxTuTx; aikamatayx. 
\num{8} (raMgaBUmi) = \hyperlink{unity pagu(3)}{unity ?pagu? \((3)\)}.

\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum

\num{2} \eng{national unity} rASeTxrXYkayx(te); rASiTxrXVya Ekate, aikamatayx. 
\hypertarget{unity pagu(3)}{} 
\num{3} \eng{the dramatic unities (the unities of time, place and action)} nATakiVya aikayxgaLu (kAleYkayx, sathxLeYkayx, kirxyeYkayx); (nATakavanunx ADalu hiDiyuva kAlavU nATakada kathe nijavAgi naDeyalu beVkAda kAlavU sarisumAru oMdeV parimiti uLaLxdAdxgiruvudu kAleYkayx, daqshayx badalAvaNe ilalxde, oTuTx kathe oMdeV sathxLadalAlxdaMte toVrisuvudu sathxLeYkayx, kathAvasutxvige neVra saMbaMdhavilalxdadxnenxlAlx biTuTx katheyanunx omumxKavAgi naDesuvudu kirxyeYkayx).

\emng

\bmng
\bnum

\num{2} tatatxvXjAcnxnavilalxda. 
\num{3} saMyama, viveVka -- ilalxda.

\emng

\num{5} takaRbadadhxvalalxda; asamaMjasavAda; doVSadiMda kUDida: \eng{an unsound argument} takaRbadadhxvalalxda vAda. 
\num{6} haguravAda; gADhavalalxda; joVralalxda: \eng{unsound slumber} haguravAda niderx.

\word{untapped} 
\pron{anfTAYxpfTx} 
\gl{\gu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\numi{1}
\banum
\alnum{a} (madayxda piVpAyi) tUtumADi horage tegeyada. 
\alnum{b} (mara) rasa tegeyada. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{2} (oMdu parxdeVsha \mo vugaLalilx) vayxvahAra beLesada; vAyxpAra hUDada; saMpakaR sAthxpisada. 
\num{3} (yAvudariMdaleV) mAhiti yA sAmagirx yA saMpanUmxlagaLanunx seLeyada, paDeyada: \eng{untapped resources} horaseLeyada, paDedukoLaLxda saMpanUmxlagaLu. 
\num{4} (keVLalu yA kare mADalu, dUravANi yA TeligArxM taMtige) sharxvaNasAdhanavanunx joVDisada, lagatitxsada. 
\enum
\emng
\eentry

\pron{anfTilf} 
\gl{\upa}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum

\num{2} (niSeVdhAthaRka racaneyalilx): \eng{he did not go until night} rAtirxyavaregU avanu hoVgalilalx. 
\num{3} (vidhuyxkatxvAda baLakeyalilx): \eng{resided there until his death} avanu tiVrihoVguvavaregU alilx vAsavAgidadx. 
\enum
\emng

\bentry

\gl{\gu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum

\bentry
\word[up(1)]{up} 
\pron{apf} 
\gl{\kirxvi}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} meVle; meVlakekx; meVlugaDe (yalilx); meVlugaDege: \eng{high up in the air} (meVle) AkAshadalilx. \eng{what are they doing up there?} alilx meVle avaru Enu mADutitxdAdxre? \eng{lives four floors up} meVle nAlakxneya aMtasitxnalilx vAsisutAtxne. \eng{went up three places in class} avanu taragatiyalilx mUru sAthxna(daSuTx) meVlakekxVrida. 
\num{2} (\AmA) alilx muMdugaDe; alilx meVlugaDe: \eng{went up front} muMdina sAlige hoVda. 
\num{3} (hiMde) yAvudoV kAladavarege. 
\num{4} nadiya meVlakekx, mUladavarege: \eng{follow a stream up to its source} nadiya meVlakekx, mUladavarege (jADu hiDidu) hoVgu. 
\num{5} oLanADinalilx. 
\num{6} (jUjukudureya savArana \vi) kudure Eri, hatitx. 
\num{7} oMdu samathaR yA kAyARtamxkavAda yA parxgatiya sithxtiyalilx yA sithxtige: \eng{stirred up trouble} samaseyx huTuTx hAkida. \eng{the house is up for sale} mane mArATakikxde. \eng{the hunt is up} beVTe yA shoVdhane shuru Agide. 
\num{8} kalitu yA tiLidu: \eng{is well up in French} pherxMcanunx cenAnxgi kalitukoMDidAdxne. 
\num{9} (rasetx \mo vugaLa \vi) ripeVriyalilx; durasitxnalilx. 
\numi{10} 
\banum
\alnum{a} (ATada gelalxMka yA sokxVrina \vi) sokxVrf boVDiRnalilx dAKale mADi, noVMdaNisi; yAvudoV oMdu samayadalilx oTuTx motatxvAgi; oMdu taMDa yA obabx ATagArana inonxMdu taMDa yA ATagArana motatxkikxMta miVrisida motatxvAgi: \eng{our team is 3 goals up} namamx taMDa mUru goVlu gaLiside yA mUru goVlugaLiMda muMdide. 
\alnum{b} (ATagArana \vi) (hAge inonxMdu taMDa yA ATagAranigiMta) hecucx gelalxMka gaLisi.

\numie
\num{11} nAyxyAlaya yA nAyxyAdhiVshana muMde hAjarupaDisi: \eng{was brought up for speeding} ati veVgavAgi ODisida kAraNakAkxgi nAyxyAlayada muMde hAjarupaDisalAyitu. 
\num{12} (\birx) (yAvudoV oMdu) bele utatxma sithxtiyalilx Eri: \eng{Rs.5 up on the transaction} (vAyxpArada) vahivATinalilx 5 rU.gaLaSuTx muMdAgi, hecAcxgi. 
\num{13} (padAthaR \mo vugaLa \vi) bele Eri: \eng{meat is up this week} I vAra mAMsada bele Eride. 
\num{14} (nATakashAleya parade) (raMgasathxLa kANisuvaMte) parade -- meVlakekx Eri, meVledudx. 
\num{15} (mAtanADuvavanu niMtiruva yA sUcisida) sathxLada yA kAladavarege baMdu, samiVpisi: \eng{the child came up and asked me the time} magu nananx baLi baMdu `eSuTx gaMTe' eMdu keVLitu. \eng{went straight up to the door} neVravAgi bAgilavarege hoVda. \eng{has been up till now} iduvarege cenAnxgi, AroVgayxvAgidAdxne. 
\numi{16} 
\banum
\alnum{a} (hAsige \mo vugaLiMda) meVlakekxdudx. 
\alnum{b} (piVThadalilx kuLitavanu, maMDiyUri kuLitavanu) meVledudx niMtu: \eng{sprang up from his seat} avanu piVThadiMda Pakakxne meVledudx niMta. 
\alnum{c} (caTuvaTikeya sUcaneyAgi) meVledudx; meVlakekx ebibxsi (modalAdAdxgi): \eng{put your umbrella up} ninanx Catirx bicicx meVletutx. 
\alnum{d} nililxsi; niMtiruva sithxtiyalilx: \eng{stood it up} adanunx nililxsida. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{17} (\BAavayx dalilx) edudxniMtu; meVlakekx niMtu. 
\num{18} parisharxma paDedu; kalitu; shikaSxNahoMdi: \eng{he is well up in mathematics} avanige gaNitadalilx oLeLxya parisharxmavide. 
\num{19} muMduvaridu; ELigeyAgi: \eng{he is up with the leaders} avanu muMduvaridu muKaMDara jate idAdxne. 
\num{20} (\nw) (cukAkxNiya \vi) gALigedurAgi. 
\num{21} daMgeyedudx. 
\num{22} (beVTe \mo vu) muMduvariyutatx; naDeyutatx. 
\num{23} (sUyaR, caMdarx, \mo vu) udayisi: \eng{the moon is up} caMdarx mUDidAdxne.

\num{25} aDakavAda, sheVKarisida yA suBadarxvAda sithxtige taMdu: \eng{pack up} poTaTxNa kaTuTx. \eng{bind up} kaTuTxgaLanAnxgi mADu. \eng{store up} sheVKara mADu. \eng{lock up} surakiSxtavAgi, BadarxvAgi -- biVga hAki BadarxpaDisu. 
\numi{26} meVlinadu eMdu BAvitavAda sathxLakekx yA sathxLadalilx, \kanmu\ 
\banum

\eanum
\numie
\num{27} sidadhxpaDisida yA apeVkiSxta sithxtige: \eng{wound up the watch} gaDiyArakekx kiVlukoTaTx. 
\num{28} (gaNakayaMtarxda \vi) naDeyutatx; baLakege sidadhxvAda.

\num{30} mugidu hoVgi; pUtiRyAgi; sigadaMtAgi: \eng{time is up} kAla mugiduhoVyitu, hotAtxyitu; veVLe miVritu. 
\num{31} hAsigeyiMda edudx: \eng{are you up yet?} niVnu inUnx edidxdidxVyA? 
\num{32} (\kanmu\ asAdhAraNavAgi yA aniriVkiSxtavAgi) naDeyatatx; Agutatx; saMBavisutatx: \eng{something is up} EnoV Agutitxde, naDeyutitxde. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} \eng{be all up with} (vayxkitxge) vinAshakaravAgi; pUtiR hAnikaravAgi; Baravase, niriVkeSx ilalxdaMte: \eng{it is all up with him} (\AmA) (nirAsheya sUcaneyAgi) avana kathe pUreYsitu. avana kathe pUtiR mugidaMteyeV. 
\num{2} \eng{something is up} (\AmA) EnoV kAdide; yAvudoV asAdhAraNavAdudu yA anapeVkiSxtavAdudu naDeyuvudaralilxde, saMBavisuvudaralilxde. 
\numi{3} \eng{up against} 
\banum
\alnum{a} hatitxravAgi; samiVpadalilx. 
\alnum{b} saMpakaRdalilx yA saMpakiRsi.

\eanum
\numie
\num{4} \eng{up against it.} (\AmA) vipariVta kaSaTxkekx sikikx. 
\num{5} \eng{up and} \hyperref{kandict_a.pdf}{A}{about(1) nuga(6)}{$^1$about} (\engit{or} \eng{doing).} 
\numi{6} \eng{up and down} 
\banum
\alnum{a} atitxtatx; alilxMdililxge; keLagiMda meVlakekx: \eng{marching up and down} atitxtatx naDedADutatx.

\numi{7} \eng{up for} 
\banum

\alnum{b} (hudedx \mo vugaLige) parigaNaneyalilxruva. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{8} \eng{up in} \hyperref{kandict_a.pdf}{A}{arms(2) nuga(5)}{$^2$arms}. 
\numi{9}\eng{up to} 
\banum
\alnum{a} varege; tanaka: \eng{up to the present} iduvarege; ililxyatanaka. 
\alnum{b} iSuTx saMKeyxya tanaka, saMKeyxya oLage: \eng{can take up to six guests} Arakekx miVradaSuTx atithigaLanunx nAnu baramADikoLaLxbalelx.

\numie
\num{10} \eng{up to} \hyperref{kandict_d.pdf}{D}{date(2) nuga(3)}{$^2$date}.

\num{17} \eng{up with (it)} (\BAavayx) (nidiRSaTx vayxkitxge yA vasutxvige beMbala sUcisuvalilx) etutx! ELu! meVlakekxtutx! jaya \mo vu Agali! adanenxtutx; adanunx meVlakekx tege: \eng{up with the Revolution!} kArxMti cirAyuvAgali! \eng{up with you} meVleVLu; edudx nilulx.

\bentry 
\word[up(2)]{up} 
\pron{apf} 
\gl{\upa}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} meVle; meVlugaDege; meVlakekx; keLaginiMda meVlinavarege: \eng{climbed up the ladder} ENiya meVle hatitxda. \eng{up the hill} beTaTxda meVlakekx. \eng{smoke goes up the chimney} hogekoLaviyalilx hoge meVleVri sAgutatxde. 
\num{2} (nadiya) mUladavarege. 
\hyperdef{U}{up(2)3}{} 
\num{3} (rasetx \mo vugaLa) udadxkUkx: \eng{walk up the street} rasetxyudadxkUkx naDe. 
\num{4} meVluBAgadalilx: \eng{lives farther up the road} rasetxyalilx inUnx savxlapx muMde, meVlugaDe vAsisutAtxne. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} \eng{sitting up a tree} marada meVleVri, tudiyalilx kuLitu. 
\num{2} \eng{up and down} (\rUpa) (yAvudoV) sathxLakekx matutx alilxMda hiMdakekx. 
\numi{3} \eng{up hill and down dale} 
\banum
\alnum{a} (parxyAsada parxyANadalilx) haLaLx tiTuTx elAlx; beTaTx hatitx kaNive iLidu. 
\alnum{b} (\rUpa) (yAvudeV saninxveVsha \mo vugaLanunx) edurisutAtx; heVgeMdare hAge naDedu koLuLxtAtx. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{4} \eng{up stage} raMgasathxLada -- hiMBAgadalilx, hiMbadiyalilx, meVluBAgadalilx. 
\num{5} \eng{up the} \hyperref{kandict_p.pdf}{P}{pole(1) pagu(2)}{$^1$pole}. 
\num{6} \eng{up the} \hyperref{kandict_s.pdf}{S}{spout(2) pagu}{$^2$spout}.

\num{1} nava shirxVmaMtanAda; idadxkikxdadxMte shirxVmaMtanAda yA meVlina adhikArakekx baMda: \eng{upstart officials in government offices} sakARri kaceVrigaLalilxna navoVnanxta adhikArigaLu. 
\numi{2} 
\banum

\bentry
\word[use(1)]{use} 
\pron{yUsfZ} 
\gl{\nA}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} baLasuvudu; upayoVgisuvudu; baLake; upayoVga; parxyoVga; viniyoVga: \eng{put it to good use} adanunx cenAnxgi upayoVgisu. \eng{has passed out of use} adu Iga baLakeyalilxlalx. \eng{is in daily use} dinabaLakeyalilxde. 
\num{2} upayoVgisuva hakukx yA shakitx yA adhikAra: \eng{lost the use of his left arm} eDatoVLanunx baLasalu avanige sAdhayxvilalx (eDatoVLanunx baLasuva shakitx kaLedukoMDidAdxne). 
\num{3} (baLasuvudara) Pala; parxyoVjana: \eng{a blunt knife is of no use} moMDa cAkuviniMda yAva parxyoVjanavU ilalx. \eng{it is no use talking} mAtanADuvudariMda, mAtanADi -- parxyoVjanavilalx. 
\num{4} padadhxti; aBAyxsa; vADike: \eng{long use has reconciled me to it} diVGaRkAlada aBAyxsadiMda nAnu adanunx sarihoMdisikoMDidedxVne. 
\num{5} (caciRna, ArAdhanA maMdirada) pUjA padadhxti; kamaRpadadhxti; dhAmiRka parxkirxyegaLu: \eng{Anglican use} iMgilxSf caciRna padadhxti. 
\num{6} (\nAyxshA) (\ca) (beVrobabx PalAnuBaviya anuBoVgakAkxgi mAtarx obabxna vashadalilxruva Asitxya) PalAnuBava; anuBoVga. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\numi{1} \eng{have no use for} 
\banum
\alnum{a} parxyoVjanavAgadiru; agatayxvilalxdiru. 
\alnum{b} (\rUpa) iSaTxvilalxdiru: kaMDare Agadiru: \eng{he had no use for laggards} avanige soVmArigaLanunx kaMDare Agadu. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{2} \eng{make use of} baLasu; upayoVgisu; parxyoVjana paDe. 
\num{3} \eng{meant for use, not for ornament} adara udedxVsha -- baLake, alaMkAravalalx. 
\num{4} \eng{use and wont} rUDhi padadhxti; sAthxpitavAda vADike. 
\enum
\emng
\eentry

\bentry
\word[use(2)]{use} 
\pron{yUsfZ} 
\gl{\sakirx}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} baLasu; upayoVgisu; parxyoVgisu; viniyoVgisu: \eng{seldom uses a knife} cAkuvanunx baLasuvudeV ilalx. \eng{use your discretion} ninanx viveVcaneyanunx upayoVgisu. 
\num{2} (hesaru \mo vanunx) savxMtakAkxgi baLasu, upayoVgisu. \eng{may I use your telephone?} nimamx dUravANiyanunx upayoVgisaleV? 
\num{3} vayxvaharisu; kANu; vatiRsu; naDeduko; naDesiko: \eng{has used me shamefully} avanu nananx bagegx avamAnakaravAgi vatiRsidAdxne. 
\num{4} (Iga \sA\ \BU\ mAtarx, \ucAcx\ yUsfTx). padadhxtiyAgiru; rUDhiyAgiru; vADikeyAgiru; aBAyxsavAgiru: \eng{I used to take the bus} nAnu basisxnalilx hoVguva rUDhi itutx. \eng{there used to be a law against it} adara virudadhxvAgi oMdu kAnUnu vADikeyalilxtutx. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum

\num{2} \eng{use force} balaparxyoVga mADu. 
\num{3} \eng{use a person's name} obabxna hesaranunx baLasiko, ulelxVKisu; obabxna hesarina parxyoVjana paDeduko.
\numi{4} \eng{use up} 
\banum
\alnum{a} (elalxvanUnx) KacuR mADibiDu; pUreYsibiDu. 
\alnum{b} (uLidiruvudanunx) upayoVgisibiDu; baLasibiDu. 
\alnum{c} (ati sharxma \mo vugaLiMda) susutx mADibiDu: \eng{he has used up all his strength} avanu tanenxlalx shakitxyanUnx kaLedukoMDu susAtxgidAdxne.

\expl{}
\bmng

\bentry

\pron{aTarf} 
\gl{\gu}
\expl{}
\bmng
(visheVSaNavAgi) saMpUNaR; tiVrA; atayxMta; kaDu; pUtiR: \eng{utter misery} daTaTxdAridarxyX; kaDukaSaTx. \eng{an utter denial} saMpUNaR nirAkaraNe. 
\emng
\eentry

\bentry
\word[utter(2)]{utter} 
\pron{aTarf} 
\gl{\sakirx}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} (suKa, duHKa, \mo vanunx) dhavxniya mUlaka -- sUcisu, vayxkatxpaDisu: \eng{utter a sigh} niTuTxsiru biDu. 
\num{2} (mAtinalilx, baravaNigeyalilx) heVLu; usuru; nuDi; ucacxrisu: \eng{the last words he uttered} avanu heVLida koneya mAtugaLu. 
\num{3} dhavxni mADu; kiricu; kUgu; moLagu: \eng{the engine uttered a shriek} eMjinunx kiVcalu dhavxnimADitu (gaTiTxyAgi kiricitu). 
\num{4} (\nAyxshA) KoVTA nANayx yA noVTu calAvaNe mADu. 
\enum
\emng
\eentry

\bentry
\word{utterance} 
\pron{aTaranfsx} 
\gl{\nA}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} heVLike; mAtinalilx vayxkatxpaDisuvudu, heVLuvudu. 
\num{2} vAkfshakitx; ucAcxraNe; mAtADuva shakitx. 
\num{3} nuDi; vacana; ukitx; BASaNa: \eng{his pulpit utterances} veVdikeya meVlina (avana) mAtugaLu, BASaNa. 
\num{4} mAtina riVti: \eng{his very utterance was spell- binding} avana mAtina riVtiyeV moVDihAkitutx. 
\num{5} (\BAshA) shabadxsaMtAna yA padasaMtAna; vAyxkaraNbadadhxvAda yAvudeV oMdu AMshika yA pUNaR GaTakavAgirabeVkAgirada, ucacxrita yA liKita padagaLa aviciPxnanx saraNi.
